The main distinguishing feature is ability to attach sound recording or photo to any data field regardless of its type. This allows to reduce data collection activity to a few short actions.\r\n\r\nThe actual data entry can be performed later, when the user can spend more time entering data into data fields in a searchable form based on media captured in the field.
